[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is classified as a heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout-of-bounds read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations and findings  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow address [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m0x50600000011f[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lies [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes past a [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte heap [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
